I've uploaded a code repository in the directory /testbed. Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
Stale Anthropic OAuth credential blocks requests after #3952 removal
## Problem

After upgrading through v2.74.0 (#3952, which removed Anthropic OAuth for TOS compliance), users who still have a `type:"oauth"` credential under `anthropic` in `auth.json` hit a hard error on every request to an Anthropic-provider model:

> Your Anthropic credentials were set up via OAuth, which is no longer supported. Please re-authenticate: run '/login', select 'Paste an API key' → Anthropic. Alternatively, switch to the Claude Code CLI provider.

This error was introduced in #4308 (commit `2dab94ad0`) as a clearer replacement for the previous generic cooldown error. However it does not clean up the stale credential, so:

- `hasAuth("anthropic")` keeps reporting true, masking the correct "no key configured" fallback.
- Users with a working local `claude` CLI can't transparently fall back — the stale OAuth entry keeps the request routed through the Anthropic provider path.
- The only remedy today is to hand-edit `auth.json`.

## Expected

When stale Anthropic OAuth is detected:

1. Self-heal: strip only the `type:"oauth"` entry, preserving any `api_key` credentials.
2. If the `claude` binary is in PATH, surface an actionable message directing the user to switch their model's provider to `claude-code`.
3. Otherwise, surface a "no key configured" style message.

## References

- Anthropic OAuth removal: #3952 / `c2acb1fb4`
- Error introduced: #4308 / `2dab94ad0`

</pr_description>

Default: SettingsManager.create(cwd, agentDir) */\n\tsettingsManager?: SettingsManager;\n\n\t/** Optional: check if the claude-code CLI provider is ready (installed + authed).\n\t * Passed to RetryHandler for third-party block recovery (#3772). */\n\tisClaudeCodeReady?: () => boolean;\n}\n\n/** Result from createAgentSession */\nexport interface CreateAgentSessionResult {\n\t/** The created session */\n\tsession: AgentSession;\n\t/** Extensions result (for UI context setup in interactive mode) */\n\textensionsResult: LoadExtensionsResult;\n\t/** Warning if session was restored with a different model than saved */\n\tmodelFallbackMessage?: string;\n}\n\n// Re-exports\n\nexport type {\n\tExtensionAPI,\n\tExtensionCommandContext,\n\tExtensionContext,\n\tExtensionFactory,\n\tSlashCommandInfo,\n\tSlashCommandLocation,\n\tSlashCommandSource,\n\tToolDefinition,\n} from \"./extensions/index.js\";\nexport type { PromptTemplate } from \"./prompt-templates.js\";\nexport type { Skill } from \"./skills.js\";\nexport type { Tool } from \"./tools/index.js\";\n\nexport {\n\t// Pre-built tools (use process.cwd())\n\treadTool,\n\tbashTool,\n\teditTool,\n\twriteTool,\n\tgrepTool,\n\tfindTool,\n\tlsTool,\n\tcodingTools,\n\treadOnlyTools,\n\tallTools as allBuiltInTools,\n\t// Tool factories (for custom cwd)\n\tcreateCodingTools,\n\tcreateReadOnlyTools,\n\tcreateReadTool,\n\tcreateBashTool,\n\tcreateEditTool,\n\tcreateWriteTool,\n\tcreateGrepTool,\n\tcreateFindTool,\n\tcreateLsTool,\n\t// Hashline edit mode\n\thashlineCodingTools,\n\thashlineEditTool,\n\thashlineReadTool,\n\tcreateHashlineCodingTools,\n\tcreateHashlineEditTool,\n\tcreateHashlineReadTool,\n};\n\n// Helper Functions\n\nfunction getDefaultAgentDir(): string {\n\treturn getAgentDir();\n}\n\n/**\n * Create an AgentSession with the specified options.\n *\n * @example\n * ```typescript\n * // Minimal - AuthStorage.create(authPath);\n\tconst modelRegistry = options.modelRegistry ?? new ModelRegistry(authStorage, modelsPath);\n\n\tconst settingsManager = options.settingsManager ?? SessionManager.create(cwd);\n\n\tif (!resourceLoader) {\n\t\tresourceLoader = new DefaultResourceLoader({ cwd, agentDir, settingsManager });\n\t\tawait resourceLoader.reload();\n\t\ttime(\"resourceLoader.reload\");\n\t}\n\n\t// Flush provider registrations queued during extension loading so that\n\t// extension models (e.g. pi-claude-cli) are visible in the registry before\n\t// findInitialModel() runs. bindCore() repeats this flush as a safety net\n\t// for any late-arriving registrations.\n\tconst { runtime: extensionRuntime } = resourceLoader.getExtensions();\n\tfor (const { name, config } of extensionRuntime.pendingProviderRegistrations) {\n\t\tmodelRegistry.registerProvider(name, config);\n\t}\n\textensionRuntime.pendingProviderRegistrations = [];\n\n\t// Check if session has existing data to restore\n\tconst existingSession = sessionManager.buildSessionContext();\n\tconst hasExistingSession = existingSession.messages.length > 0;\n\tconst hasThinkingEntry = sessionManager.getBranch().some((entry) => entry.type === \"thinking_level_change\");\n\n\tlet model = options.model;\n\tlet modelFallbackMessage: string | undefined;\n\n\t// If session has data, try to restore model from it\n\tif (!model && hasExistingSession && existingSession.model) {\n\t\tconst restoredModel = modelRegistry.find(existingSession.model.provider, existingSession.model.modelId);\n\t\tif (restoredModel && (await modelRegistry.getApiKey(restoredModel))) {\n\t\t\tmodel = restoredModel;\n\t\t}\n\t\tif (!model) {\n\t\t\tmodelFallbackMessage = `Could not restore model ${existingSession.model.provider}/${existingSession.model.modelId}`;\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Flush extension provider registrations so extension-provided models (e.g. claude-code/*)\n\t// are available in the registry before model resolution. Without this, findInitialModel()\n\t// cannot find extension models and falls back to built-in providers (#3534).\n\tconst extensionsForModelResolution = resourceLoader.getExtensions();\n\tfor (const { name, config } of extensionsForModelResolution.runtime.pendingProviderRegistrations) {\n\t\tmodelRegistry.registerProvider(name, config);\n\t}\n\t// Clear the queue so bindCore() doesn't re-register the same providers.\n\textensionsForModelResolution.runtime.pendingProviderRegistrations = [];\n\n\t// If still no model, use findInitialModel (checks settings default, then provider defaults)\n\tif (!model) {\n\t\tconst result = await findInitialModel({\n\t\t\tscopedModels: [],\n\t\t\tisContinuing: hasExistingSession,\n\t\t\tdefaultProvider: settingsManager.getDefaultProvider(),\n\t\t\tdefaultModelId: settingsManager.getDefaultModel(),\n\t\t\tdefaultThinkingLevel: settingsManager.getDefaultThinkingLevel(),\n\t\t\tmodelRegistry,\n\t\t});\n\t\tmodel = result.model;\n\t\tif (!model) {\n\t\t\tmodelFallbackMessage = `No models available. Use /login or set an API key environment variable. See ${join(getDocsPath(), \"providers.md\")}. Then use /model to select a model.`;\n\t\t} else if (modelFallbackMessage) {\n\t\t\tmodelFallbackMessage += `. Using ${model.provider}/${model.id}`;\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tlet thinkingLevel = options.thinkingLevel;\n\n\t// If session has data, restore thinking level from it\n\tif (thinkingLevel === undefined && hasExistingSession) {\n\t\tthinkingLevel = hasThinkingEntry\n\t\t\t? (existingSession.thinkingLevel as ThinkingLevel)\n\t\t\t: (settingsManager.getDefaultThinkingLevel() ?? DEFAULT_THINKING_LEVEL);\n\t}\n\n\t// Fall back to settings default\n\tif (thinkingLevel === undefined) {\n\t\tthinkingLevel = settingsManager.getDefaultThinkingLevel() ?? DEFAULT_THINKING_LEVEL;\n\t}\n\n\t// Clamp to model capabilities\n\tif (!model || !model.reasoning) {\n\t\tthinkingLevel = \"off\";\n\t}\n\n\tconst editMode = settingsManager.getEditMode();\n\tconst defaultActiveToolNames: ToolName[] = editMode === \"hashline\"\n\t\t? === \"image\" ? { type: \"text\" as const, text: \"Image reading is disabled.\" } : c,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t)\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t.filter(\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t(c, i, arr) =>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t// Dedupe consecutive \"Image reading is disabled.\" texts\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t!(\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tc.type === \"text\" &&\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tc.text === \"Image reading is disabled.\" &&\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\ti > 0 &&\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tarr[i - 1].type === \"text\" &&\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t(arr[i - 1] as { type: \"text\"; text: string }).text === \"Image reading is disabled.\"\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t);\n\t\t\t\t\t\treturn { ...msg, content: filteredContent };\n\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\treturn msg;\n\t\t});\n\t};\n\n\tconst mid-turn.\n\t\t\tconst resolvedProvider = provider || agent.state.model?.provider;\n\t\t\tif (!resolvedProvider) {\n\t\t\t\tthrow new Error(\"No model selected\");\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tconst authMode = modelRegistry.getProviderAuthMode(resolvedProvider);\n\t\t\tif (authMode === \"externalCli\" || authMode === \"none\") {\n\t\t\t\treturn undefined;\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t// Retry key resolution with backoff to handle transient network failures\n\t\t\t// (e.g., OAuth token refresh failing due to brief connectivity loss).\n\t\t\t// When credentials are in a cooldown window (e.g., after a 429), wait\n\t\t\t// for the backoff to expire instead of using fixed delays that are\n\t\t\t// shorter than the cooldown duration.\n\t\t\tconst maxAttempts = 3;\n\t\t\tconst baseDelayMs = 2000;\n\t\t\tconst maxCooldownWaitMs = 60_000; // Don't wait longer than 60s (skip quota-exhausted 30min backoffs)\n\t\t\tfor (let attempt = 1; attempt <= maxAttempts; attempt++) {\n\t\t\t\tconst key = await modelRegistry.getApiKeyForProvider(resolvedProvider);\n\t\t\t\tif (key) return key;\n\n\t\t\t\t// On the last attempt, fall through to error handling below\n\t\t\t\tif (attempt >= maxAttempts) break;\n\n\t\t\t\t// Only retry if credentials exist (network issue) — no point retrying\n\t\t\t\t// when there are genuinely no credentials configured.\n\t\t\t\tconst hasAuth = modelRegistry.authStorage.hasAuth(resolvedProvider);\n\t\t\t\tconst model = agent.state.model;\n\t\t\t\tconst isOAuth = model && modelRegistry.isUsingOAuth(model);\n\t\t\t\tif (!hasAuth && !isOAuth)      1	/**
     2	 * Credential storage for API keys and OAuth tokens.
     3	 * Handles loading, saving, and refreshing credentials from auth.json.
     4	 *
     5	 * Supports multiple credentials per provider with round-robin selection,
     6	 * session-sticky hashing, and automatic rate-limit fallback.
     7	 *
     8	 * Uses file locking to prevent race conditions when multiple pi instances
     9	 * try to refresh tokens simultaneously.
    10	 */
    11	
    12	import {
    13	        getEnvApiKey,
    14	        type OAuthCredentials,
    15	        type OAuthLoginCallbacks,
    16	        type OAuthProviderId,
    17	} from "@gsd/pi-ai";
    18	import { getOAuthApiKey, getOAuthProvider, getOAuthProviders } from "@gsd/pi-ai/oauth";
    19	import { chmodSync, existsSync, mkdirSync, readFileSync, writeFileSync } from "fs";
    20	import { dirname, join } from "path";
    21	import { getAgentDir } from "../config.js";
    22	import { AUTH_LOCK_STALE_MS } from "./constants.js";
    23	import { acquireLockAsync, acquireLockSyncWithRetry } from "./lock-utils.js";
    24	import { resolveConfigValue } from "./resolve-config-value.js";
    25	
    26	export type ApiKeyCredential = {
    27	        type: "api_key";
    28	        key: string;
    29	};
    30	
    31	export type OAuthCredential = {
    32	        type: "oauth";
    33	} & OAuthCredentials;
    34	
    35	export type AuthCredential = ApiKeyCredential | OAuthCredential;
    36	
    37	// ============================================================================
    38	// Google OAuth token detection
    39	// ============================================================================
    40	
    41	/**
    42	 * Providers that use Google AI Studio API keys (not OAuth tokens).
    43	 * OAuth access tokens (ya29.*) are not valid API keys for these providers.
    44	 */
    45	const GOOGLE_API_KEY_PROVIDERS = new Set(["google"]);
    46	
    47	/**
    48	 * Detect if a string is a Google OAuth access token rather than an API key.
    49	 * Google OAuth access tokens start with "ya29." — these are issued by
    50	 * Google's OAuth2 token endpoint and are not valid as AI Studio API keys.
    51	 *
    52	 * Users who installed Google's Gemini CLI may have these tokens and
    53	 * mistakenly set them as GEMINI_API_KEY.
    54	 */
    55	export function isGoogleOAuthToken(key: string): boolean {
    56	        return key.startsWith("ya29.");
    57	}
    58	
    59	/**
    60	 * Validate that an API key is not a Google OAuth token being used for
    61	 * a provider that requires actual API keys (e.g., Google AI Studio).
    62	 * Throws a descriptive error if the key appears to be an OAuth token.
    63	 */
    64	function validateNotGoogleOAuthToken(provider: string, key: string): void {
    65	        if (GOOGLE_API_KEY_PROVIDERS.has(provider) && isGoogleOAuthToken(key)) {
    66	                throw new Error(
    67	                        `The provided key for "${provider}" appears to be a Google OAuth access token (ya29.*), ` +
    68	                                `not a valid API key. Google AI Studio requires an API key starting with "AIza...". ` +
    69	                                `\n\nIf you're using Google's Gemini CLI, its OAuth tokens are not compatible. ` +
    70	                                `Either:\n` +
    71	                                `  1. Get an API key from https://aistudio.google.com/apikey and set GEMINI_API_KEY\n` +
    72	                                `  2. Use '/login google-gemini-cli' to authenticate via Cloud Code Assist`,
    73	                );
    74	        }
    75	}
    76	
    77	/**
    78	 * On-disk format: each provider maps to a single credential or an array of credentials.
    79	 * Single credentials are normalized to arrays at load time for internal use.
    80	 */
    81	export type AuthStorageData = Record<string, AuthCredential | AuthCredential[]>;
    82	
    83	type LockResult<T> = {
    84	        result: T;
    85	        next?: string;
    86	};
    87	
    88	export interface AuthStorageBackend {
    89	        withLock<T>(fn: (current: string | undefined) => LockResult<T>): T;
    90	        withLockAsync<T>(fn: (current: string | undefined) => Promise<LockResult<T>>): Promise<T>;
    91	}
    92	
    93	export class FileAuthStorageBackend implements AuthStorageBackend {
    94	        constructor(private authPath: string = join(getAgentDir(), "auth.json")) {}
    95	
    96	        private ensureParentDir(): void {
    97	                const dir = dirname(this.authPath);
    98	                if (!existsSync(dir)) {
    99	                        mkdirSync(dir, { recursive: true, mode: 0o700 });
   100	                }
   101	        }
   102	
   103	        private ensureFileExists(): void {
   104	                if (!existsSync(this.authPath)) {
   105	                        writeFileSync(this.authPath, "{}", "utf-8");
   106	                        chmodSync(this.authPath, 0o600);
   107	                }
   108	        }
   109	
   110	        withLock<T>(fn: (current: string | undefined) => LockResult<T>): T {
   111	                this.ensureParentDir();
   112	                this.ensureFileExists();
   113	
   114	                let release: (() => void) | undefined;
   115	                try {
   116	                        release = acquireLockSyncWithRetry(this.authPath);
   117	                        const current = existsSync(this.authPath) ? readFileSync(this.authPath, "utf-8") : undefined;
   118	                        const { result, next } = fn(current);
   119	                        if (next !== undefined) {
   120	                                writeFileSync(this.authPath, next, "utf-8");
   121	                                chmodSync(this.authPath, 0o600);
   122	                        }
   123	                        return result;
   124	                } finally {
   125	                        if (release) {
   126	                                release();
   127	                        }
   128	                }
   129	        }
   130	
   131	        async withLockAsync<T>(fn: (current: string | undefined) => Promise<LockResult<T>>): Promise<T> {
   132	                this.ensureParentDir();
   133	                this.ensureFileExists();
   134	
   135	                let release: (() => Promise<void>) | undefined;
   136	                let lockCompromised = false;
   137	                let lockCompromisedError: Error | undefined;
   138	                const throwIfCompromised = () => {
   139	                        if (lockCompromised) {
   140	                                throw lockCompromisedError ?? new Error("Auth storage lock was compromised");
   141	                        }
   142	                };
   143	
   144	                try {
   145	                        release = await acquireLockAsync(this.authPath, {
   146	                                staleMs: AUTH_LOCK_STALE_MS,
   147	                                onCompromised: (err) => {
   148	                                        lockCompromised = true;
   149	                                        lockCompromisedError = err;
   150	                                },
   151	                        });
   152	
   153	                        throwIfCompromised();
   154	                        const current = existsSync(this.authPath) ? readFileSync(this.authPath, "utf-8") : undefined;
   155	                        const { result, next } = await fn(current);
   156	                        throwIfCompromised();
   157	                        if (next !== undefined) {
   158	                                writeFileSync(this.authPath, next, "utf-8");
   159	                                chmodSync(this.authPath, 0o600);
   160	                        }
   161	                        throwIfCompromised();
   162	                        return result;
   163	                } finally {
   164	                        if (release) {
   165	                                try {
   166	                                        await release();
   167	                                } catch {
   168	                                        // Ignore unlock errors when lock is compromised.
   169	                                }
   170	                        }
   171	                }
   172	        }
   173	}
   174	
   175	export class InMemoryAuthStorageBackend implements AuthStorageBackend {
   176	        private value: string | undefined;
   177	
   178	        withLock<T>(fn: (current: string | undefined) => LockResult<T>): T {
   179	                const { result, next } = fn(this.value);
   180	                if (next !== undefined) {
   181	                        this.value = next;
   182	                }
   183	                return result;
   184	        }
   185	
   186	        async withLockAsync<T>(fn: (current: string | undefined) => Promise<LockResult<T>>): Promise<T> {
   187	                const { result, next } = await fn(this.value);
   188	                if (next !== undefined) {
   189	                        this.value = next;
   190	                }
   191	                return result;
   192	        }
   193	}
   194	
   195	// ============================================================================
   196	// Backoff durations for different error types (milliseconds)
   197	// ============================================================================
   198	
   199	const BACKOFF_RATE_LIMIT_MS = 30_000; // 30s for rate limit / 429
   200	const BACKOFF_QUOTA_EXHAUSTED_MS = 30 * 60_000; // 30min for quota exhausted
   201	const BACKOFF_SERVER_ERROR_MS = 20_000; // 20s for 5xx server errors
   202	const BACKOFF_DEFAULT_MS = 60_000; // 60s fallback
   203	
   204	export type UsageLimitErrorType = "rate_limit" | "quota_exhausted" | "server_error" | "unknown";
   205	
   206	/**
   207	 * Get backoff duration for an error type.
   208	 */
   209	function getBackoffDuration(errorType: UsageLimitErrorType): number {
   210	        switch (errorType) {
   211	                case "rate_limit":
   212	                        return BACKOFF_RATE_LIMIT_MS;
   213	                case "quota_exhausted":
   214	                        return BACKOFF_QUOTA_EXHAUSTED_MS;
   215	                case "server_error":
   216	                        return BACKOFF_SERVER_ERROR_MS;
   217	                default:
   218	                        return BACKOFF_DEFAULT_MS;
   219	        }
   220	}
   221	
   222	/**
   223	 * Simple string hash for session-sticky credential selection.
   224	 * Returns a positive integer.
   225	 */
   226	function hashString(str: string): number {
   227	        let hash = 0;
   228	        for (let i = 0; i < str.length; i++) {
   229	                const char = str.charCodeAt(i);
   230	                hash = ((hash << 5) - hash + char) | 0;
   231	        }
   232	        return Math.abs(hash);
   233	}
   234

   368	                if (this.loadError) {

   396	        /**
   397	         * Set credential for a provider. For API key credentials, appends to
   398	         * existing credentials (accumulation on duplicate login). For OAuth,
   399	         * replaces (only one OAuth token per provider makes sense).
   400	         */
   401	        set(provider: string, credential: AuthCredential): void {
   402	                if (credential.type === "api_key") {
   403	                        // Block Google OAuth tokens being stored as API keys for AI Studio providers
   404	                        validateNotGoogleOAuthToken(provider, credential.key);
   405	
   406	                        const existing = this.getCredentialsForProvider(provider);
   407	                        // Deduplicate: don't add if same key already exists
   408	                        const isDuplicate = existing.some(
   409	                                (c) => c.type === "api_key" && c.key === credential.key,
   410	                        );
   411	                        if (isDuplicate) return;
   412	
   413	                        const updated = [...existing, credential];
   414	                        this.data[provider] = updated.length === 1 ? updated[0] : updated;
   415	                        this.persistProviderChange(provider, updated.length === 1 ? updated[0] : updated);
   416	                } else {
   417	                        // OAuth: replace any existing OAuth credential, keep API keys
   418	                        const existing = this.getCredentialsForProvider(provider);
   419	                        const apiKeys = existing.filter((c) => c.type === "api_key");
   420	                        if (apiKeys.length === 0) {
   421	                                this.data[provider] = credential;
   422	                                this.persistProviderChange(provider, credential);
   423	                        } else {
   424	                                const updated = [...apiKeys, credential];
   425	                                this.data[provider] = updated;
   426	                                this.persistProviderChange(provider, updated);
   427	                        }
   428	                }
   429	        }

   526	        areAllCredentialsBackedOff(provider: string): boolean {

   539	        markProviderExhausted(provider: string, errorType: UsageLimitErrorType): void {
   540	                const backoffMs = getBackoffDuration(errorType);
   541	                this.providerBackoff.set(provider, Date.now() + backoffMs);

   543	
   544	        /**
   545	         * Check if a provider is currently available (not backed off at provider level).
   546	         */
   547	        isProviderAvailable(provider: string): boolean {
   548	                const expiresAt = this.providerBackoff.get(provider);
   549	                if (expiresAt === undefined) return true;
   550	                if (Date.now() >= expiresAt) {
   551	                        this.providerBackoff.delete(provider);
   552	                        return true;
   553	                }
   554	                return false;
   555	        }
   556	
   557	        /**
   558	         * Get milliseconds remaining until provider backoff expires.
   559	         * Returns 0 if provider is available.
   560	         */
   561	        getProviderBackoffRemaining(provider: string): number {
   562	                const expiresAt = this.providerBackoff.get(provider);
   563	                if (expiresAt === undefined) return 0;
   564	                const remaining = expiresAt - Date.now();
   565	                if (remaining <= 0) {
   566	                        this.providerBackoff.delete(provider);
   567	                        return 0;
   568	                }
   569	                return remaining;
   570	        }
   571	
   572	        /**
   573	         * Get the earliest timestamp at which any credential for this provider
   574	         * will become available again.  Returns `undefined` when no credentials
   575	         * are backed off (i.e. all are immediately available).
   576	         *
   577	         * Callers can use this to sleep exactly long enough for the cooldown to
   578	         * clear instead of using a fixed retry delay that may be shorter than the
   579	         * backoff window.
   580	         */
   581	        getEarliestBackoffExpiry(provider: string): number | undefined {
   582	                const providerMap = this.credentialBackoff.get(provider);
   583	                if (!providerMap || providerMap.size === 0) return undefined;
   584	
   585	                const now = Date.now();
   586	                let earliest: number | undefined;
   587	
   588	                for (const [index, expiresAt] of providerMap) {
   589	                        if (expiresAt <= now) {
   590	                                // Already expired — clean up
   591	                                providerMap.delete(index);
   592	                                continue;
   593	                        }
   594	                        if (earliest === undefined || expiresAt < earliest) {
   595	                                earliest = expiresAt;
   596	                        }
   597	                }
   598	
   599	                return earliest;
   600	        }
   601	
   602	        /**
   603	         * Check if a credential index is currently backed off.
   604	         */
   605	        private isCredentialBackedOff(provider: string, index: number): boolean {
   606	                const providerBackoff = this.credentialBackoff.get(provider);
   607	                if (!providerBackoff) return false;
   608	                const expiresAt = providerBackoff.get(index);
   609	                if (expiresAt === undefined) return false;
   610	                if (Date.now() >= expiresAt) {
   611	                        providerBackoff.delete(index);
   612	                        return false;
   613	                }
   614	                return true;
   615	        }

   620	         * - Otherwise, uses round-robin as the starting point.
   621	         * - Skips credentials that are currently backed off.
   622	         * - Returns -1 if all credentials are backed off.
   623	         */
   624	        private selectCredentialIndex(provider: string, credentials: AuthCredential[], sessionId?: string): number {
   625	                if (credentials.length === 0) return -1;
   626	                if (credentials.length === 1) {
   627	                        return this.isCredentialBackedOff(provider, 0) ? -1 : 0;
   628	                }
   629	
   630	                let startIndex: number;
   631	                if (sessionId) {
   632	                        startIndex = hashString(sessionId) % credentials.length;
   633	                } else {
   634	                        const current = this.providerRoundRobinIndex.get(provider) ?? 0;
   635	                        startIndex = current % credentials.length;
   636	                        this.providerRoundRobinIndex.set(provider, current + 1);
   637	                }
   638	
   639	                // Try starting from the preferred index, wrapping around
   640	                for (let offset = 0; offset < credentials.length; offset++) {
   641	                        const index = (startIndex + offset) % credentials.length;
   642	                        if (!this.isCredentialBackedOff(provider, index)) {
   643	                                return index;
   644	                        }
   645	                }
   646	
   647	                // All credentials are backed off
   648	                return -1;
   649	        }
   650	
   651	        /**
   652	         * Mark a credential as rate-limited. Finds the credential that was most
   653	         * recently used for this provider+session and backs it off.
   654	         *
   655	         * @returns true if another credential is available (caller should retry),
   656	         *          false if all credentials for this provider are backed off.
   657	         */
   658	        markUsageLimitReached(
   659	                provider: string,
   660	                sessionId?: string,
   661	                options?: { errorType?: UsageLimitErrorType },
   662	        ): boolean {
   663	                const credentials = this.getCredentialsForProvider(provider);
   664	                if (credentials.length === 0) return false;
   665	
   666	                const errorType = options?.errorType ?? "rate_limit";
   667	
   668	                // For unknown/transport errors (e.g. connection reset, "terminated"),
   669	                // don't back off the only credential — it would make getApiKey() return
   670	                // undefined and surface a misleading "Authentication failed" message.
   671	                if (errorType === "unknown" && credentials.length === 1) {
   672	                        return false;
   673	                }
   674	
   675	                const backoffMs = getBackoffDuration(errorType);
   676	
   677	                // Determine which credential was just used (same logic as selectCredentialIndex
   678	                // but without incrementing round-robin)
   679	                let usedIndex: number;
   680	                if (credentials.length === 1) {
   681	                        usedIndex = 0;
   682	                } else if (sessionId) {
   683	                        usedIndex = hashString(sessionId) % credentials.length;
   684	                } else {
   685	                        // Round-robin was already incremented in getApiKey, so the last-used
   686	                        // index is (current - 1). Note: in a concurrent scenario where another
   687	                        // getApiKey call fires between the original request and this backoff call,
   688	                        // we may back off the wrong credential index. This is acceptable because:
   689	                        // (a) pi runs single-threaded event loop, (b) backing off the wrong key
   690	                        // is safe — it self-heals when the backoff expires.
   691	                        const current = this.providerRoundRobinIndex.get(provider) ?? 0;
   692	                        usedIndex = ((current - 1) % credentials.length + credentials.length) % credentials.length;
   693	                }
   694	
   695	                // Set backoff for this credential
   696	                let providerBackoff = this.credentialBackoff.get(provider);
   697	                if (!providerBackoff) {
   698	                        providerBackoff = new Map();
   699	                        this.credentialBackoff.set(provider, providerBackoff);
   700	                }
   701	                providerBackoff.set(usedIndex, Date.now() + backoffMs);
   702	
   703	                // Check if any credential is still available
   704	                for (let i = 0; i < credentials.length; i++) {
   705	                        if (!this.isCredentialBackedOff(provider, i)) {
   706	                                return true;
   707	                        }
   708	                }
   709	                return false;
   710	        }

   712	        /**
   713	         * Refresh OAuth token with backend locking to prevent race conditions.
   714	         * Multiple pi instances may try to refresh simultaneously when tokens expire.
   715	         */
   716	        private async refreshOAuthTokenWithLock(
   717	                providerId: OAuthProviderId,
   718	        ): Promise<{ apiKey: string; newCredentials: OAuthCredentials } | null> {
   719	                const provider = getOAuthProvider(providerId);
   720	                if (!provider) {
   721	                        return null;
   722	                }
   723	
   724	                const result = await this.storage.withLockAsync(async (current) => {
   725	                        const currentData = this.parseStorageData(current);
   726	                        this.data = currentData;
   727	                        this.loadError = null;
   728	
   729	                        // Find the OAuth credential for this provider
   730	                        const creds = this.getCredentialsForProvider(providerId);
   731	                        const cred = creds.find((c) => c.type === "oauth");
   732	                        if (!cred || cred.type !== "oauth") {
   733	                                return { result: null };
   734	                        }
   735	
   736	                        if (Date.now() < cred.expires) {
   737	                                return { result: { apiKey: provider.getApiKey(cred), newCredentials: cred } };
   738	                        }
   739	
   740	                        const oauthCreds: Record<string, OAuthCredentials> = {};
   741	                        for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(currentData)) {
   742	                                const first = Array.isArray(value) ? value.find((c) => c.type === "oauth") : value;
   743	                                if (first?.type === "oauth") {
   744	                                        oauthCreds[key] = first;
   745	                                }
   746	                        }
   747	
   748	                        const refreshed = await getOAuthApiKey(providerId, oauthCreds);
   749	                        if (!refreshed) {
   750	                                return { result: null };
   751	                        }
   752	
   753	                        // Update the OAuth credential in-place within the array
   754	                        const existingEntry = currentData[providerId];
   755	                        const newOAuthCred: OAuthCredential = { type: "oauth", ...refreshed.newCredentials };
   756	                        let updatedEntry: AuthCredential | AuthCredential[];
   757	
   758	                        if (Array.isArray(existingEntry)) {
   759	                                updatedEntry = existingEntry.map((c) => (c.type === "oauth" ? newOAuthCred : c));
   760	                        } else {
   761	                                updatedEntry = newOAuthCred;
   762	                        }
   763	
   764	                        const merged: AuthStorageData = {
   765	                                ...currentData,
   766	                                [providerId]: updatedEntry,
   767	                        };
   768	                        this.data = merged;
   769	                        this.loadError = null;
   770	                        return { result: refreshed, next: JSON.stringify(merged, null, 2) };
   771	                });
   772	
   773	                // Notify listeners after credential change (e.g., model registry refresh)
   774	                if (result) {
   775	                        queueMicrotask(() => this.notifyCredentialChange());
   776	                }
   777	
   778	                return result;
   779	        }

   782	         * Resolve an API key from a single credential.
   783	         */
   784	        private async resolveCredentialApiKey(
   785	                providerId: string,
   786	                cred: AuthCredential,
   787	        ): Promise<string | undefined> {
   788	                if (cred.type === "api_key") {
   789	                        return resolveConfigValue(cred.key);
   790	                }
   791	
   792	                if (cred.type === "oauth") {
   793	                        const provider = getOAuthProvider(providerId);
   794	                        if (!provider) return undefined;
   795	
   796	                        const needsRefresh = Date.now() >= cred.expires;
   797	                        if (needsRefresh) {
   798	                                try {
   799	                                        const result = await this.refreshOAuthTokenWithLock(providerId);
   800	                                        if (result) return result.apiKey;
   801	                                } catch (error) {
   802	                                        this.recordError(error);
   803	                                        this.reload();
   804	                                        const updatedCreds = this.getCredentialsForProvider(providerId);
   805	                                        const updatedOAuth = updatedCreds.find((c) => c.type === "oauth");
   806	                                        if (updatedOAuth?.type === "oauth" && Date.now() < updatedOAuth.expires) {
   807	                                                return provider.getApiKey(updatedOAuth);
   808	                                        }
   809	                                        return undefined;
   810	                                }
   811	                        } else {
   812	                                return provider.getApiKey(cred);
   813	                        }
   814	                }
   815	
   816	                return undefined;
   817	        }

   819	        /**
   820	         * Get API key for a provider.
   821	         * Priority:
   822	         * 1. Runtime override (CLI --api-key)
   823	         * 2. Credential(s) from auth.json (with round-robin / session-sticky selection)
   824	         * 3. Environment variable
   825	         * 4. Fallback resolver (models.json custom providers)
   826	         *
   827	         * @param providerId - The provider to get an API key for
   828	         * @param sessionId - Optional session ID for sticky credential selection
   829	         */
   830	        async getApiKey(providerId: string, sessionId?: string, options?: { baseUrl?: string }): Promise<string | undefined> {
   831	                // If the model has a local baseUrl, return a dummy key to avoid auth blocking
   832	                if (options?.baseUrl && !this.fallbackResolver?.(providerId)) {
   833	                        try {
   834	                                const hostname = new URL(options.baseUrl).hostname;
   835	                                if (hostname === "localhost" || hostname === "127.0.0.1" || hostname === "0.0.0.0" || hostname === "::1") {
   836	                                        return "local-no-key-needed";
   837	                                }
   838	                        } catch {
   839	                                if (options.baseUrl.startsWith("unix:")) {
   840	                                        return "local-no-key-needed";
   841	                                }
   842	                        }
   843	                }
   844	
   845	                // Runtime override takes highest priority
   846	                const runtimeKey = this.runtimeOverrides.get(providerId);
   847	                if (runtimeKey) {
   848	                        // Block Google OAuth tokens used as runtime API key overrides
   849	                        if (GOOGLE_API_KEY_PROVIDERS.has(providerId) && isGoogleOAuthToken(runtimeKey)) {
   850	                                this.recordError(
   851	                                        new Error(
   852	                                                `Blocked Google OAuth access token (ya29.*) for provider "${providerId}". ` +
   853	                                                        `Use an API key from https://aistudio.google.com/apikey or '/login google-gemini-cli'.`,
   854	                                        ),
   855	                                );
   856	                                return undefined;
   857	                        }
   858	                        return runtimeKey;
   859	                }
   860	
   861	                const credentials = this.getCredentialsForProvider(providerId);
   862	
   863	                if (credentials.length > 0) {
   864	                        const index = this.selectCredentialIndex(providerId, credentials, sessionId);
   865	                        if (index >= 0) {
   866	                                const resolved = await this.resolveCredentialApiKey(providerId, credentials[index]);
   867	                                if (resolved) return resolved;
   868	                                // Credential unresolvable (e.g. type:"oauth" for a non-OAuth provider) —
   869	                                // fall through to env / fallback instead of returning undefined (#2083)
   870	                        }
   871	                        // All credentials backed off or unresolvable - fall through to env/fallback
   872	                }
   873	
   874	                // Fall back to environment variable
   875	                const envKey = getEnvApiKey(providerId);
   876	                if (envKey) {
   877	                        // Block Google OAuth tokens from environment variables (e.g., GEMINI_API_KEY=ya29.*)
   878	                        if (GOOGLE_API_KEY_PROVIDERS.has(providerId) && isGoogleOAuthToken(envKey)) {
   879	                                this.recordError(
   880	                                        new Error(
   881	                                                `GEMINI_API_KEY contains a Google OAuth access token (ya29.*), not an API key. ` +
   882	                                                        `Get an API key from https://aistudio.google.com/apikey or use '/login google-gemini-cli'.`,
   883	                                        ),
   884	                                );
   885	                                return undefined;
   886	                        }
   887	                        return envKey;
   888	                }
   889	
   890	                // Fall back to custom resolver (e.g., models.json custom providers)
   891	                return this.fallbackResolver?.(providerId) ?? undefined;
   892	        }

   895	         * Get all registered OAuth providers
   896	         */

   898	                return getOAuthProviders();

Here's the result of running `cat -n` on /testbed/src/resources/extensions/claude-code-cli/readiness.ts:
     1	/**
     2	 * Readiness check for the Claude Code CLI provider.
     3	 *
     4	 * Verifies the `claude` binary is installed, responsive, AND authenticated.
     5	 * Results are cached for 30 seconds to avoid shelling out on every
     6	 * model-availability check.
     7	 *
     8	 * Auth verification follows the T3 Code pattern: run `claude auth status`
     9	 * and check the exit code + output for an authenticated session.
    10	 */
    11	
    12	import { execFileSync } from "node:child_process";
    13	
    14	let cachedBinaryPresent: boolean | null = null;
    15	let cachedAuthed: boolean | null = null;
    16	let lastCheckMs = 0;
    17	const CHECK_INTERVAL_MS = 30_000;
    18	
    19	function refreshCache(): void {
    20	        const now = Date.now();
    21	        if (cachedBinaryPresent !== null && now - lastCheckMs < CHECK_INTERVAL_MS) {
    22	                return;
    23	        }
    24	
    25	        // Set timestamp first to prevent re-entrant checks during the same window
    26	        lastCheckMs = now;
    27	
    28	        // Check binary presence
    29	        try {
    30	                execFileSync("claude", ["--version"], { timeout: 5_000, stdio: "pipe" });
    31	                cachedBinaryPresent = true;
    32	        } catch {
    33	                cachedBinaryPresent = false;
    34	                cachedAuthed = false;
    35	                return;
    36	        }
    37	
    38	        // Check auth status — exit code 0 with non-error output means authenticated
    39	        try {
    40	                const output = execFileSync("claude", ["auth", "status"], { timeout: 5_000, stdio: "pipe" })
    41	                        .toString()
    42	                        .toLowerCase();
    43	                // The CLI outputs "not logged in", "no credentials", or similar when unauthenticated
    44	                cachedAuthed = !(/not logged in|no credentials|unauthenticated|not authenticated/i.test(output));
    45	        } catch {
    46	                // Non-zero exit code means not authenticated
    47	                cachedAuthed = false;
    48	        }
    49	}
    50	
    51	/**
    52	 * Whether the `claude` binary is installed (regardless of auth state).
    53	 */
    54	export function isClaudeBinaryPresent(): boolean {
    55	        refreshCache();
    56	        return cachedBinaryPresent ?? false;
    57	}
    58	
    59	/**
    60	 * Whether the `claude` CLI is authenticated with a valid session.
    61	 * Returns false if the binary is not installed.
    62	 */
    63	export function isClaudeCodeAuthed(): boolean {
    64	        refreshCache();
    65	        return (cachedBinaryPresent ?? false) && (cachedAuthed ?? false);
    66	}
    67	
    68	/**
    69	 * Full readiness check: binary installed AND authenticated.
    70	 * This is the gating function used by the provider registration.
    71	 */
    72	export function isClaudeCodeReady(): boolean {
    73	        refreshCache();
    74	        return (cachedBinaryPresent ?? false) && (cachedAuthed ?? false);
    75	}
    76	
    77	/**
    78	 * Force-clear the cached readiness state.
    79	 * Useful after the user completes auth setup so the next check is fresh.
    80	 */
    81	export function clearReadinessCache(): void {
    82	        cachedBinaryPresent = null;
    83	        cachedAuthed = null;
    84	        lastCheckMs = 0;
    85	}
    86

   144	/** Result of loading custom models from models.json */

   147	        /** Providers with baseUrl/headers/apiKey overrides for built-in models */
   148	        overrides: Map<string, ProviderOverride>;

   157	
   158	function mergeCompat(
   159	        baseCompat: Model<Api>["compat"],
   160	        overrideCompat: ModelOverride["compat"],
   161	): Model<Api>["compat"] | undefined {
   162	        if (!overrideCompat) return baseCompat;
   163	
   164	        const base = baseCompat as OpenAICompletionsCompat | OpenAIResponsesCompat | undefined;
   165	        const override = overrideCompat as OpenAICompletionsCompat | OpenAIResponsesCompat;
   166	        const merged = { ...base, ...override } as OpenAICompletionsCompat | OpenAIResponsesCompat;
   167	
   168	        const baseCompletions = base as OpenAICompletionsCompat | undefined;
   169	        const overrideCompletions = override as OpenAICompletionsCompat;
   170	        const mergedCompletions = merged as OpenAICompletionsCompat;
   171	
   172	        if (baseCompletions?.openRouterRouting || overrideCompletions.openRouterRouting) {
   173	                mergedCompletions.openRouterRouting = {
   174	                        ...baseCompletions?.openRouterRouting,
   175	                        ...overrideCompletions.openRouterRouting,
   176	                };
   177	        }
   178	
   179	        if (baseCompletions?.vercelGatewayRouting || overrideCompletions.vercelGatewayRouting) {
   180	                mergedCompletions.vercelGatewayRouting = {
   181	                        ...baseCompletions?.vercelGatewayRouting,
   182	                        ...overrideCompletions.vercelGatewayRouting,
   183	                };
   184	        }
   185	
   186	        return merged as Model<Api>["compat"];
   187	}
   188	
   189	/**
   190	 * Deep merge a model override into a model.
   191	 * Handles nested objects (cost, compat) by merging rather than replacing.
   192	 */
   193	function applyModelOverride(model: Model<Api>, override: ModelOverride): Model<Api> {
   194	        const result = { ...model };
   195	
   196	        // Simple field overrides
   197	        if (override.name !== undefined) result.name = override.name;
   198	        if (override.reasoning !== undefined) result.reasoning = override.reasoning;
   199	        if (override.input !== undefined) result.input = override.input as ("text" | "image")[];
   200	        if (override.contextWindow !== undefined) result.contextWindow = override.contextWindow;
   201	        if (override.maxTokens !== undefined) result.maxTokens = override.maxTokens;
   202	
   203	        // Merge cost (partial override)
   204	        if (override.cost) {
   205	                result.cost = {
   206	                        input: override.cost.input ?? model.cost.input,
   207	                        output: override.cost.output ?? model.cost.output,
   208	                        cacheRead: override.cost.cacheRead ?? model.cost.cacheRead,
   209	                        cacheWrite: override.cost.cacheWrite ?? model.cost.cacheWrite,
   210	                };
   211	        }
   212	
   213	        // Merge headers
   214	        if (override.headers) {
   215	                const resolvedHeaders = resolveHeaders(override.headers);
   216	                result.headers = resolvedHeaders ? { ...model.headers, ...resolvedHeaders } : model.headers;
   217	        }
   218	
   219	        // Deep merge compat
   220	        result.compat = mergeCompat(model.compat, override.compat);
   221	
   222	        return result;
   223	}
   224

   226	/**
   227	 * Model registry - loads and manages models, resolves API keys via AuthStorage.
   228	 */
   229	export class ModelRegistry {
   230	        private models: Model<Api>[] = [];
   231	        private discoveredModels: Model<Api>[] = [];
   232	        private discoveryCache: ModelDiscoveryCache;
   233	        private customProviderApiKeys: Map<string, string> = new Map();
   234	        private registeredProviders: Map<string, ProviderConfigInput> = new Map();
   235	        private loadError: string | undefined = undefined;
   236	
   237	        constructor(
   238	                readonly authStorage: AuthStorage,
   239	                readonly modelsJsonPath: string | undefined = join(getAgentDir(), "models.json"),
   240	        ) {
   241	                this.discoveryCache = new ModelDiscoveryCache();
   242	
   243	                // Set up fallback resolver for custom provider API keys
   244	                this.authStorage.setFallbackResolver((provider) => {
   245	                        const keyConfig = this.customProviderApiKeys.get(provider);
   246	                        if (keyConfig) {
   247	                                return resolveConfigValue(keyConfig);
   248	                        }
   249	                        return getEnvApiKey(provider);
   250	                });
   251	
   252	                // Refresh models when credentials change (e.g., OAuth token refresh with new model limits)

   541	         * Get auth mode for a provider.

   543	         */
   544	        getProviderAuthMode(provider: string): ProviderAuthMode {
   545	                const config = this.registeredProviders.get(provider);
   546	                if (!config) return "apiKey";
   547	                if (config.authMode) return config.authMode;
   548	                if (config.oauth) return "oauth";
   549	                if (config.apiKey) return "apiKey";
   550	                return "apiKey";
   551	        }

   553	        /**
   554	         * Whether a provider can be used for requests/fallback without hard auth gating.
   555	         */
   556	        isProviderRequestReady(provider: string): boolean {
   557	                const config = this.registeredProviders.get(provider);
   558	                if (config?.isReady) return config.isReady();
   559	                const authMode = this.getProviderAuthMode(provider);
   560	                if (authMode === "externalCli" || authMode === "none") return true;
   561	                return this.authStorage.hasAuth(provider);
   562	        }

	/**
	 * Remove only legacy OAuth credentials for a provider, preserving any API keys.
	 * Returns true when at least one OAuth credential was removed.
	 */
	removeLegacyOAuthCredential(provider: string): boolean {
		const existing = this.getCredentialsForProvider(provider);
		if (!existing.some((c) => c.type === "oauth")) return false;

		const updated = existing.filter((c) => c.type !== "oauth");
		if (updated.length === 0) {
			delete this.data[provider];
			this.persistProviderChange(provider, undefined);
		} else {
			const next = updated.length === 1 ? updated[0] : updated;
			this.data[provider] = next;
			this.persistProviderChange(provider, next);
		}

		this.providerRoundRobinIndex.delete(provider);
		this.credentialBackoff.delete(provider);
		this.providerBackoff.delete(provider);
		queueMicrotask(() => this.notifyCredentialChange());
		return true;
	}

		try {
			const removed = this.storage.withLock((current) => {
				const currentData = this.parseStorageData(current);
				const entry = currentData[provider];
				const existing = !entry ? [] : Array.isArray(entry) ? entry : [entry];
				if (!existing.some((c) => c.type === "oauth")) {
					this.data = currentData;
					this.loadError = null;
					return { result: false };
				}

				const updated = existing.filter((c) => c.type !== "oauth");
				const merged: AuthStorageData = { ...currentData };
				if (updated.length === 0) {
					delete merged[provider];
				} else {
					merged[provider] = updated.length === 1 ? updated[0] : updated;
				}

				this.data = merged;
				this.loadError = null;
				return { result: true, next: JSON.stringify(merged, null, 2) };
			});

			this.credentialBackoff.delete(provider);
			this.providerBackoff.delete(provider);

			return true;
		} catch (error) {

+        withLock<T>(fn: (current: string | undefined) => LockResult<T>): T {
+                this.ensureParentDir();
+                this.ensureFileExists();
+
+                let release: (() => void) | undefined;
+                try {
+                        release = acquireLockSyncWithRetry(this.authPath);
+                        const current = existsSync(this.authPath) ? readFileSync(this.authPath, "utf-8") : undefined;
+                        const { result, next } = fn(current);
+                        if (next !== undefined) {

+        async withLockAsync<T>(fn: (current: string | undefined) => Promise<LockResult<T>>): Promise<T> {
+                this.ensureParentDir();
+                this.ensureFileExists();
+
+                let release: (() => Promise<void>) | undefined;
+                let lockCompromised = false;
+                let lockCompromisedError: Error | undefined;
+                const throwIfCompromised = () => {
+                        if (lockCompromised) {
+                                throw lockCompromisedError ?? new Error("Auth storage lock was compromised");
+                        }
+                };
+
+                try {
+                        release = await acquireLockAsync(this.authPath, {
+                                staleMs: AUTH_LOCK_STALE_MS,
+                                onCompromised: (err) => {
+                                        lockCompromised = true;
+                                        lockCompromisedError = err;
+                                },
+                        });
+
+                        throwIfCompromised();
+                        const current = existsSync(this.authPath) ? readFileSync(this.authPath, "utf-8") : undefined;
+                        const { result, next } = await fn(current);
+                        throwIfCompromised();
+                        if (next !== undefined) {
+                                writeFileSync(this.authPath, next, "utf-8");
+                                chmodSync(this.authPath, 0o600);
+                        }
+                        throwIfCompromised();
+                        return result;
+                } finally {
+                        if (release) {
+                                try {
+                                        await release();
+                                } catch {
+                                        // Ignore unlock errors when lock is compromised.
+                                }
+                        }
+                }
+        }
